[Clinician]
It’s great that you’re reflecting on how you feel about decision-making. It’s common to feel stuck in a loop of second-guessing. One helpful approach is to consider a few strategies:

1. **Clarify Your Values**: Understanding what matters most to you can help guide your decisions. What are your priorities right now in life or work?

2. **Set Boundaries for Decision-Making**: Give yourself a time limit to make a decision. This can help prevent overthinking. You might say, “I’ll take 10 minutes to decide on this.”

3. **Pros and Cons**: Writing down a list of the pros and cons for each option can help visualize your choices and can sometimes clarify what you truly want.

4. **Practice Self-Compassion**: Remind yourself that it’s okay to make mistakes. Every decision is an opportunity for growth and learning.

5. **Talk it Out**: Since you prefer discussing things, talking through your options with someone you trust may provide new perspectives and reduce the weight of the decision.

How do these strategies resonate with you?

**Here’s a short exercise we can try:**

1. **Find a comfortable position:** You can either sit or stand, whatever feels best for you.
  
2. **Take a deep breath in through your nose:** Count to four as you inhale, filling your lungs completely.

5. **Repeat this a couple of times:** Inhale for four, hold for four, and exhale for six. With each breath, notice if there's any change in how you're feeling or any tension you might be holding.
